The changes between the\\n89:    API versions are listed in libsanitizer/asan/asan_interface_internal.h.\\n90: \\n91:    The run-time library redefines malloc (so that redzone are inserted around\\n92:    the allocated memory) and free (so that reuse of free-ed memory is delayed),\\n93:    provides __asan_report* and __asan_init_vN functions.\\n94: \\n95:    Read more:\\n96:    http://code.google.com/p/address-sanitizer/wiki/AddressSanitizerAlgorithm\\n97: \\n98:    The current implementation supports detection of out-of-bounds and\\n99:    use-after-free in the heap, on the stack and for global variables.\\n100: \\n101: \",\"url\":\"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333@baaf9b33ef307e3d2752a94e62274c374e6a5e20/-/blob/gcc/asan.cc%3FL1-100\"}","structuredContent":{"content":"1: /* AddressSanitizer, a fast memory error detector.\n2:    Copyright (C) 2012-2026 Free Software Foundation, Inc.\n3:    Contributed by Kostya Serebryany <kcc@google.com>\n4: \n5: This file is part of GCC.\n6: \n7: GCC is free software; you can redistribute it and/or modify it under\n8: the terms of the GNU General Public License as published by the Free\n9: Software Foundation; either version 3, or (at your option) any later\n10: version.\n11: \n12: GCC is distributed in the hope that it will be useful, but WITHOUT ANY\n13: WARRANTY; without even the implied warranty of MERCHANTABILITY or\n14: FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE.  // *(short*) for 16-byte access.\n78:        if (ShadowValue)\n79: \t __asan_report_load8(X);\n80:      For a load of N bytes (N=1, 2 or 4) from address X:\n81:        ShadowAddr = (X >> 3) + Offset\n82:        ShadowValue = *(char*)ShadowAddr;\n83:        if (ShadowValue)\n84: \t if ((X & 7) + N - 1 > ShadowValue)\n85: \t   __asan_report_loadN(X);\n86:    Stores are instrumented similarly, but using __asan_report_storeN functions.\n87:    A call too __asan_init_vN() is inserted to the list of module CTORs.\n88:    N is the version number of the AddressSanitizer API. The changes between the\n89:    API versions are listed in libsanitizer/asan/asan_interface_internal.h.\n90: \n91:    The run-time library redefines malloc (so that redzone are inserted around\n92:    the allocated memory) and free (so that reuse of free-ed memory is delayed),\n93:    provides __asan_report* and __asan_init_vN functions.\n94: \n95:    Read more:\n96:    http://code.google.com/p/address-sanitizer/wiki/AddressSanitizerAlgorithm\n97: \n98:    The current implementation supports detection of out-of-bounds and\n99:    use-after-free in the heap, on the stack and for global variables.\n100: \n101: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333@baaf9b33ef307e3d2752a94e62274c374e6a5e20/-/blob/gcc/asan.cc%3FL1-100"}}}
